
# Warming Up

http://www.pythonchallenge.com/pc/def/0.html

线索：试着改变URL的地址-->把图片中得到的数字输入到URL中


```python
print(2**38)
```

    274877906944
    

# What about making trans

http://www.pythonchallenge.com/pc/def/map.html

线索：想要解开它，你需要想2次--> K-M,O-Q,E-G 每个字母都往后推了2次


```python
def transmes(mes):
    intab = 'abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz'
    outtab ='cdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyzab'
    trantab = str.maketrans(intab,outtab)
    message = mes.translate(trantab) 
    print(message)

message = "g fmnc wms bgblr rpylqjyrc gr zw fylb. rfyrq ufyr amknsrcpq ypc dmp. bmgle gr gl zw fylb gq glcddgagclr ylb rfyr'q ufw rfgq rcvr gq qm jmle. sqgle qrpgle.kyicrpylq() gq pcamkkclbcb. lmu ynnjw ml rfc spj."
transmes(message)
url = 'map'
transmes(url)
```

    i hope you didnt translate it by hand. thats what computers are for. doing it in by hand is inefficient and that's why this text is so long. using string.maketrans() is recommended. now apply on the url.
    ocr
    

希望你没有一个一个去推算字母解密这段话，这样的工作应该是由电脑来做。手动推送很费时，所以这段话会如此之长。推荐用 string.maketrans() 方法来解密这道题，现在把它应用在url上。

# ocr

http://www.pythonchallenge.com/pc/def/ocr.html

线索：找出字母。他们可能在书中，可能在页面源码上。-->查看源代码，看注释，在下面这堆乱七八糟的信息中，找到出现次数最少的字母

```python
%&]!{{%*_!*}&)}$**_{*!#%[[#]!](^^$![#[[*}%(_#^^!%))!_^@)@**@}}(%%{#*%@(((]^%^![&
}!)$]&($)@](+(#{$)_%^%_^^#][{*[)%}+[##(##^{$}^]#&(&*{)%)&][&{]&#]}[[^^&[!#}${@_(
#@}&$[[%]_&$+)$!%{(}$^$}*'''
```


```python
def count_char(mes): 
    infos = {}
    for i in mes:
        if i.isalpha():
            if i not in infos:
                infos[i] = 0
                infos[i] += 1
    a  = sorted(infos.items(),key = lambda item:item[1])[0:10]
    print(a)

count_char(page_message)
```

    [('e', 1), ('q', 1), ('u', 1), ('a', 1), ('l', 1), ('i', 1), ('t', 1), ('y', 1)]
    

# re

http://www.pythonchallenge.com/pc/def/equality.html

线索：一个小写字母的两边准确地被3个大写字母包围 --> 那么它的格式就是 xXXXxXXXx

```python
import re

pattern = r'[a-z][A-Z]{3}[a-z][A-Z]{3}[a-z]'
for i in re.findall(pattern,mes3):
    print(i[4],end='')
```

    linkedlist

# follow the chain

http://www.pythonchallenge.com/pc/def/linkedlist.php

线索：打开源代码，注释中 --> urllib 可能有帮助。千万不要把所有的 NOTHING 都试一遍，因为它不会停，400 次完全够了


```python
import requests
import re
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup
url = 'http://www.pythonchallenge.com/pc/def/linkedlist.php'
data = requests.get(url)
soup = BeautifulSoup(data.text,'lxml')
href = soup.a['href']
p = re.search(r'(\d)+$',href).group()

i = 0
while(True):
    next_url = url + '?nothing=' + str(p)
    next_page = requests.get(next_url).text
    print(str(i)+":"+ next_page,p)
    if re.search(r'two',next_page):
        p =int(p)/2
    elif (re.search(r'(\d)+$',next_page)):
        p = re.search(r'(\d)+$',next_page).group()
    else:
        break 
    i += 1
```
